 To turn on background polynonmial fits...
 Make file "creaminpar_bg.par" in target light curve directory
 structured like...
 Nppoly - integer of order of polynomial
 
 polyin(1:NPpoly) the coeffs of the polynomial fit, start at zero so background
 is just flat line equal to mean of light curve.
 
 polyin_step(1:Nppoly,ilc) - stepsizes set to -1 to let code guess
 polyin_pri(1:Nppoly,ilc) - Gaussian priors on polynomial coefficients

 To turn on background polynonmial fits...
 Make file "creaminpar_bg.par" in target light curve directory
 structured like...
 Nppoly - integer of order of polynomial
 
 polyin(1:NPpoly) the coeffs of the polynomial fit, start at zero so background
 is just flat line equal to mean of light curve.
 
 polyin_step(1:Nppoly,ilc) - stepsizes set to -1 to let code guess
 polyin_pri(1:Nppoly,ilc) - Gaussian priors on polynomial coefficients
